
namespace = sarc_char_design

sarc_char_design.1001 = {
	type = character_event
	title = sarc_char_design.1001.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = { has_game_rule = sarc_initial_five }
				desc = sarc_char_design.1001.desc.5
			}
			desc = sarc_char_design.1001.desc.10
		}
	}
	theme = family
	override_background = { reference = bedchamber }
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_bold
	}

	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = sarc_char_design_point_system_50
				}
				custom_tooltip = sarc.design.points.50
				set_variable = {
					name = design_points
					value = 50
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = sarc_char_design_point_system_75
				}
				custom_tooltip = sarc.design.points.75
				set_variable = {
					name = design_points
					value = 75
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = sarc_char_design_point_system_100
				}
				custom_tooltip = sarc.design.points.100
				set_variable = {
					name = design_points
					value = 100
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = sarc.design.points.25
				set_variable = {
					name = design_points
					value = 25
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = sarc_initial_five
				}
				set_variable = {
					name = design_martial
					value = 5
				}
				set_variable = {
					name = design_stewardship
					value = 5
				}
				set_variable = {
					name = design_diplomacy
					value = 5
				}
				set_variable = {
					name = design_intrigue
					value = 5
				}
				set_variable = {
					name = design_learning
					value = 5
				}
				set_variable = {
					name = design_prowess
					value = 5
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = {
					name = design_martial
					value = 10
				}
				set_variable = {
					name = design_stewardship
					value = 10
				}
				set_variable = {
					name = design_diplomacy
					value = 10
				}
				set_variable = {
					name = design_intrigue
					value = 10
				}
				set_variable = {
					name = design_learning
					value = 10
				}
				set_variable = {
					name = design_prowess
					value = 10
				}
			}
		}
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.9998
	}

	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.no
	}
}

sarc_char_design.1002 = {
	type = character_event
	title = sarc_char_design.1002.choice.t
	desc = sarc_char_design.1002.choice.desc
	theme = family
	override_background = { reference = courtyard }
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_bold
	}

	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.age.random
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.1003
	}

	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.age.child
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_female = no
			}
			trigger_event = sarc_char_design.1004
		}
		else = {
			trigger_event = sarc_char_design.1005
		}
	}
}

sarc_char_design.1003 = {
	type = character_event
	title = sarc_char_design.age.event.t
	desc = sarc_char_design.age.event.d
	theme = family
	override_background = { reference = courtyard }
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_bold
	}

	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.age.16
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = age_2
				has_character_flag = age_3
				has_character_flag = age_4
				has_character_flag = age_5
				has_character_flag = age_6
				has_character_flag = age_7
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = sarc_initial_five
				}
				create_character = {
					employer = root
					gender_female_chance = 0
					random_traits = no
					age = 16
					diplomacy = 5
					martial = 5
					stewardship = 5
					intrigue = 5
					learning = 5
					prowess = 5
					health = 5.0
					fertility = 0.6
					save_scope_as = custom_char
					set_variable = { name = sarc_custom_char_var value = this }
					
					dynasty = root
					faith = root.faith
					culture = root.culture
				}
				set_variable = { name = sarc_custom_char_var value = scope:custom_char }
			}
			else = {
				create_character = {
					employer = root
					gender_female_chance = 0
					random_traits = no
					age = 16
					diplomacy = 10
					martial = 10
					stewardship = 10
					intrigue = 10
					learning = 10
					prowess = 10
					health = 5.0
					fertility = 0.6
					save_scope_as = custom_char
					set_variable = { name = sarc_custom_char_var value = this }
					
					dynasty = root
					faith = root.faith
					culture = root.culture
				}
				set_variable = { name = sarc_custom_char_var value = scope:custom_char }
			}
			set_designated_heir = var:sarc_custom_char_var
		}
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.9997
	}

	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.age.17
		trigger = {

	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.age.more
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_2
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_2
			add_character_flag = age_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_3
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_3
			add_character_flag = age_4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_4
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_4
			add_character_flag = age_5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_5
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_5
			add_character_flag = age_6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_6
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_6
			add_character_flag = age_7
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_7
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_7
		}
		else = {
			add_character_flag = age_2
		}
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.1003
	}
}

sarc_char_design.1004 = {
	type = character_event
	title = sarc_char_design.age.event.t
	desc = sarc_char_design.age.event.d
	theme = default
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_bold
	}

	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.age.16
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = age_2
				has_character_flag = age_3
				has_character_flag = age_4
				has_character_flag = age_5
				has_character_flag = age_6
				has_character_flag = age_7
			}
			age >= 17
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = sarc_initial_five
				}
				create_character = {
					employer = root
					gender_female_chance = 0
					random_traits = no
					age = 16
					diplomacy = 5
					martial = 5
					stewardship = 5
					intrigue = 5
					learning = 5
					prowess = 5
					health = 5.0
					fertility = 0.6
					father = root
					save_scope_as = custom_char
					set_variable = { name = sarc_custom_char_var value = this }
					
					dynasty = root
					faith = root.faith
					culture = root.culture
				}
				set_variable = { name = sarc_custom_char_var value = scope:custom_char }
			}
			else = {
				create_character = {
					employer = root
					gender_female_chance = 0
					random_traits = no
					age = 16
					diplomacy = 10
					martial = 10
					stewardship = 10
					intrigue = 10
					learning = 10
					prowess = 10
					health = 5.0
					fertility = 0.6
					father = root
					save_scope_as = custom_char
					set_variable = { name = sarc_custom_char_var value = this }
					
					dynasty = root
					faith = root.faith
					culture = root.culture
				}
				set_variable = { name = sarc_custom_char_var value = scope:custom_char }
			}
			set_designated_heir = var:sarc_custom_char_var
		}
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.9997
	}

	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.age.more
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_2
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_2
			add_character_flag = age_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_3
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_3
			add_character_flag = age_4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_4
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_4
			add_character_flag = age_5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_5
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_5
			add_character_flag = age_6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_6
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_6
			add_character_flag = age_7
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_7
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_7
		}
		else = {
			add_character_flag = age_2
		}
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.1004
	}
}

sarc_char_design.1005 = {
	type = character_event
	title = sarc_char_design.age.event.t
	desc = sarc_char_design.age.event.d
	theme = default
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_bold
	}

	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.age.16
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = age_2
				has_character_flag = age_3
				has_character_flag = age_4
				has_character_flag = age_5
				has_character_flag = age_6
				has_character_flag = age_7
			}
			age >= 17
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = sarc_initial_five
				}
				create_character = {
					employer = root
					gender_female_chance = 0
					random_traits = no
					age = 16
					diplomacy = 5
					martial = 5
					stewardship = 5

					has_game_rule = sarc_initial_five
				}

					faith = root.faith
					culture = root.culture
				}

			}

					has_game_rule = sarc_initial_five
				}
				create_character = {
					employer = root
					gender_female_chance = 0
					random_traits = no
					age = 5
					diplomacy = 5
					martial = 5
					stewardship = 5
					intrigue = 5
					learning = 5
					prowess = 5
					health = 5.0
					fertility = 0.6
					mother = root
					save_scope_as = custom_char
					set_variable = { name = sarc_custom_char_var value = this }
					
					dynasty = root
					faith = root.faith
					culture = root.culture
				}
				set_variable = { name = sarc_custom_char_var value = scope:custom_char }
			}
			else = {
				create_character = {
					employer = root

	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.age.more
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_2
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_2
			add_character_flag = age_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_3
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_3
			add_character_flag = age_4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_4
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_4
			add_character_flag = age_5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_5
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_5
			add_character_flag = age_6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_6
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_6
			add_character_flag = age_7
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_7
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_7
		}
		else = {
			add_character_flag = age_2
		}
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.1005
	}
}

sarc_char_design.2005 = {
	type = character_event
	title = sarc_char_design.age.event.t
	desc = sarc_char_design.age.event.d
	theme = default
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_bold
	}

	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.age.16
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = age_2
				has_character_flag = age_3
				has_character_flag = age_4
				has_character_flag = age_5
				has_character_flag = age_6
				has_character_flag = age_7
			}
			age >= 17
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = sarc_initial_five
				}
				create_character = {
					employer = root
					gender_female_chance = 100
					random_traits = no
					age = 16
					diplomacy = 5
					martial = 5
					stewardship = 5
					intrigue = 5
					learning = 5
					prowess = 5
					health = 5.0
					fertility = 0.6
					mother = root
					save_scope_as = custom_char
					set_variable = { name = sarc_custom_char_var value = this }
					
					dynasty = root
					faith = root.faith
					culture = root.culture
				}
				set_variable = { name = sarc_custom_char_var value = scope:custom_char }
			}
			else = {
				create_character = {
					employer = root
					gender_female_chance = 100
					random_traits = no
					age = 16
					diplomacy = 10
					martial = 10
					stewardship = 10
					intrigue = 10
					learning = 10
					prowess = 10
					health = 5.0
					fertility = 0.6

	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.age.more
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_2
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_2
			add_character_flag = age_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_3
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_3
			add_character_flag = age_4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_4
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_4
			add_character_flag = age_5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_5
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_5
			add_character_flag = age_6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_6
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_6
			add_character_flag = age_7
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_7
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_7
		}
		else = {
			add_character_flag = age_2
		}
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.2005
	}
}

sarc_char_design.1008 = {
	type = character_event
	title = sarc_char_design.skill.event.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = { has_game_rule = sarc_initial_five }
				desc = sarc_char_design.skill.event.d.5
			}
			desc = sarc_char_design.skill.event.d.10
		}
	}
	theme = default
	left_portrait = {
		character = var:sarc_custom_char_var
		animation = personality_bold
	}

	option = {
		name = martial
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.1011
	}

	option = {
		name = diplomacy
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.1012
	}

	option = {
		name = stewardship
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.1013
	}

	option = {
		name = intrigue
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.1014
	}

	option = {
		name = learning
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.1015
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system
		}
		name = prowess
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.1016
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			trigger = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system }
			text = sarc_char_design.back.menu
		}
		name = {
			trigger = { NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system } }
			text = sarc_char_design.back.menu.points
		}
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.9999
	}
}

sarc_char_design.1011 = {
	type = character_event
	title = sarc_char_design.martial.event.t
	desc = sarc_char_design.martial.event.d
	theme = default
	left_portrait = {
		character = var:sarc_custom_char_var
		animation = personality_bold
	}

	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.skill.add1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system } 
					var:design_points >= 1
				}
			}
		}
		var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
			add_martial_skill = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system }
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = design_points
				subtract = 1
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = design_martial
				add = 1
			}
			custom_tooltip = sarc.design.points.subtract.1
		}

sarc_char_design.1023 = {
	type = character_event
	title = sarc_char_design.traits.personality.event.t
	desc = sarc_char_design.traits.personality.event.d
	theme = default
	left_portrait = {
		character = var:sarc_custom_char_var
		animation = personality_bold
	}

	option = {
		name = trait_lustful
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system
				var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
					has_trait = lustful
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system } 
					var:design_points >= 3
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
					has_trait = chaste
				}
			}
		}
		var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = lustful
				}
				remove_trait = lustful
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system }
					}
					root = {
						change_variable = {
							name = design_points
							add = 3
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = sarc.design.points.add.3
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_trait = lustful
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system }
					}
					root = {
						change_variable = {
							name = design_points
							subtract = 3
						}
					}	
					custom_tooltip = sarc.design.points.subtract.3
				}
			}
		}
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.1023

		name = trait_chaste

				}
			}

					}
					root = {

							name = design_points
							subtract = 2
						}
					}	
					custom_tooltip = sarc.design.points.subtract.2
				}
			}
		}
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.1023
	}

				limit = {
					has_trait = gluttonous
				}
				remove_trait = gluttonous
				if = {
					limit = {

					limit = {

				var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
					has_trait = ambitious
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system } 
					var:design_points >= 5
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
					has_trait = content
				}
			}
		}
		var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = ambitious
				}
				remove_trait = ambitious
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system }
					}
					root = {
						change_variable = {
							name = design_points
							add = 5
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = sarc.design.points.add.5
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_trait = ambitious
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system }
					}
					root = {
						change_variable = {
							name = design_points
							subtract = 5
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = sarc.design.points.subtract.5
				}
			}
		}
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.1025
	}

	option = {

			OR = {

				var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
					has_trait = athletic
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system } 
					var:design_points >= 2
				}
			}
		}
		var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = athletic
				}
				remove_trait = athletic
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system }
					}
					root = {
						change_variable = {
							name = design_points
							add = 2
						}

					custom_tooltip = sarc.design.points.add.2
				}

sarc_char_design.1031 = {
	type = character_event
	title = sarc_char_design.traits.beauty.event.t
	desc = sarc_char_design.traits.beauty.event.d
	theme = default
	left_portrait = {
		character = var:sarc_custom_char_var
		animation = personality_bold
	}

	option = {
		name = trait_beauty_bad_1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system
				AND = {
					var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
						has_trait = beauty_bad_1
					}
					NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system } 
					var:design_points >= 1
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system } 
					NOT = {
						var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
							has_trait = beauty_bad_1
						}
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = beauty_good_1
						has_trait = beauty_good_2
						has_trait = beauty_good_3
					}
				}
			}
		}

				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system }

					root = {
						change_variable = {
							name = design_points
							subtract = 1
						}

		var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = dull
				}
				remove_trait = dull
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system }
					}
					root = {
						change_variable = {
							name = design_points
							subtract = 10
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = sarc.design.points.subtract.10
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_trait = dull
				if = {
					limit = {

		var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = military_engineer
				}
				remove_trait = military_engineer
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system }
					}
					root = {
						change_variable = {
							name = design_points
							add = 3
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = sarc.design.points.add.3
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_trait = military_engineer
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system }
					}
					root = {
						change_variable = {
							name = design_points
							subtract = 3
						}
					}

sarc_char_design.1122 = {
	type = character_event
	title = sarc_char_design.education.event2.t
	desc = sarc_char_design.education.event2.d
	theme = default
	left_portrait = {
		character = var:sarc_custom_char_var
		animation = personality_bold
	}

	option = {
		name = trait_education_martial_1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system
				var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
					has_trait = education_martial_1
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system } 
					var:design_points >= 2
				}
			}
		}
		var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = education_martial_1
				}
				remove_trait = education_martial_1
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system }
					}
					root = {
						change_variable = {
							name = design_points
							add = 2
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = sarc.design.points.add.2
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_trait = education_martial_1
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system }
					}
					root = {
						change_variable = {
							name = design_points
							subtract = 2

				}

		name = sarc_char_design.age.more
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_2
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_2
			add_character_flag = age_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_3
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_3
			add_character_flag = age_4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_4
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_4
			add_character_flag = age_5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_5
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_5
			add_character_flag = age_6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_6
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_6
			add_character_flag = age_7
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_7
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_7
		}
		else = {
			add_character_flag = age_2
		}
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.2003
	}
}

			}
			age >= 24

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = sarc_initial_five
				}
				create_character = {
					employer = root
					gender_female_chance = 100
					random_traits = no
					age = 12
					diplomacy = 5
					martial = 5
					stewardship = 5
					intrigue = 5
					learning = 5
					prowess = 5
					health = 5.0
					fertility = 0.6
					father = root
					save_scope_as = custom_char
					set_variable = { name = sarc_custom_char_var value = this }
					
					dynasty = root
					faith = root.faith
					culture = root.culture
				}
				set_variable = { name = sarc_custom_char_var value = scope:custom_char }
			}
			else = {
				create_character = {
					employer = root
					gender_female_chance = 100
					random_traits = no
					age = 12
					diplomacy = 10
					martial = 10
					stewardship = 10
					intrigue = 10
					learning = 10
					prowess = 10
					health = 5.0
					fertility = 0.6
					father = root
					save_scope_as = custom_char
					set_variable = { name = sarc_custom_char_var value = this }
					
					dynasty = root
					faith = root.faith
					culture = root.culture
				}
				set_variable = { name = sarc_custom_char_var value = scope:custom_char }
			}
			set_designated_heir = var:sarc_custom_char_var
			var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = sarc_char_design.9995
					days = 1465
				}			
			}
		}
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.9997
	}

	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.age.13
		trigger = {

					id = sarc_char_design.9995
					days = 370
				}

		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.9997
	}
	
	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.age.more
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_2
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_2
			add_character_flag = age_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_3
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_3
			add_character_flag = age_4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_4
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_4
			add_character_flag = age_5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_5
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_5
			add_character_flag = age_6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_6
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_6
			add_character_flag = age_7
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = age_7
			}
			remove_character_flag = age_7
		}
		else = {
			add_character_flag = age_2
		}
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.2004
	}
}

	}

sarc_char_design.3001 = {
	type = character_event
	title = sarc_char_design.traits.lifestyle.event.t
	desc = sarc_char_design.traits.physique.event.d
	theme = default
	left_portrait = {
		character = var:sarc_custom_char_var
		animation = personality_bold
	}

	option = {
		name = trait_diplomat
		trigger = {
			var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
				has_character_flag = lifestyle_trait_cycle_1
			}
			OR = {
				has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system
				var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
					has_trait = diplomat
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system } 
					var:design_points >= 5
				}
			}
		}
		var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = diplomat
				}
				remove_trait = diplomat
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system }
					}
					root = {
						change_variable = {
							name = design_points
							add = 5
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = sarc.design.points.add.5
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_trait = diplomat
				if = {
					limit = {

			remove_character_flag = lifestyle_trait_cycle_4
		}
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.1020
	}
}

		character = var:sarc_custom_char_var
		animation = personality_bold
	}

	option = {
		name = trait_celibate
		trigger = {
			var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
				has_character_flag = other_trait_cycle_1
			}
			OR = {
				has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system
				var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
					has_trait = celibate
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system } 
					var:design_points >= 0
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = reveler_1
						has_trait = reveler_2
						has_trait = reveler_3
						has_trait = seducer
					}
				}
			}
		}
		var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = celibate
				}
				remove_trait = celibate
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system }
					}
					
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_trait = celibate
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system }
					}
					
				}
			}
		}
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.3002
	}

					has_trait = viking
				}
				remove_trait = viking
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system }
					}
					root = {
						change_variable = {
							name = design_points
							add = 3
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = sarc.design.points.add.3
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_trait = viking
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_game_rule = no_sarc_char_design_point_system }
					}
					root = {
						change_variable = {
							name = design_points
							subtract = 3
						}
					}	
					custom_tooltip = sarc.design.points.subtract.3
				}
			}
		}
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.3002
	}

sarc_char_design.9002 = {
	type = character_event
	title = sarc_char_design.appearance.weight.t
	desc = sarc_char_design.appearance.desc
	theme = default
	left_portrait = {
		character = var:sarc_custom_char_var
		animation = personality_bold
	}
	
	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.appearance.weight.cycle_up
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_6
				}
			}
		}
		var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_6
				}
				remove_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_6
				add_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_5
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_5
				}
				remove_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_5
				add_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_4
				}
				remove_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_4
				add_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_3
				}
				remove_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_3
				add_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_2
				}
				remove_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_2
				add_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_1
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_1
				}
				remove_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_1
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_1
				}
				remove_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_1
				add_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_2
				}
				remove_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_2
				add_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_3
				}
				remove_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_3
				add_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_4
				}
				remove_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_4
				add_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_5
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_5
				}
				remove_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_5
				add_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_6
			}
			else = {
				add_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_1
			}
		}
		trigger_event = sarc_char_design.9002
	}

	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.appearance.weight.cycle_down
		trigger = {
			var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_6
				}
			}
		}
		var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
			if = {

				add_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_4

					has_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_4
				}

				add_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_3
				}
				remove_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_3
				add_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_2
				}
				remove_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_2
				add_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_1
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_1
				}
				remove_character_flag = sarc_overweight_flag_1
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_1
				}
				remove_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_1
				add_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_2
			}
			else_if = {

					has_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_2
				}
				remove_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_2
				add_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_3
			}
			else_if = {

					has_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_3

				remove_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_3
				add_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_4

			else_if = {

					has_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_4

				add_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_5
			}
			else_if = {

				}
				remove_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_5
				add_character_flag = sarc_underweight_flag_6

				limit = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_height_down_flag_6

			}

				limit = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_height_up_flag_9

				add_character_flag = sarc_height_up_flag_10
			}
			else = {
				add_character_flag = sarc_height_up_flag_1

	}

	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.height.cycle_down
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
					has_character_flag = sarc_height_down_flag_11
				}
			}
		}

			if = {

sarc_char_design.1080 = {
	type = character_event
	title = sarc_char_design.finish.event.t
	desc = sarc_char_design.finish.event.d
	theme = default
	left_portrait = {
		character = var:sarc_custom_char_var
		animation = personality_bold
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			# Ensure the new character is the designated heir
			set_designated_heir = var:sarc_custom_char_var
			# Sync faith/culture
			var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
				set_character_faith = root.faith
				set_culture = root.culture
				# Copy racial traits for LOTR/AGOT compatibility
				if = { limit = { root = { has_trait = trait_race_elf } } add_trait = trait_race_elf }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_trait = trait_race_dwarf } } add_trait = trait_race_dwarf }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_trait = trait_race_orc } } add_trait = trait_race_orc }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_trait = trait_race_hobbit } } add_trait = trait_race_hobbit }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_trait = trait_race_uruk_hai } } add_trait = trait_race_uruk_hai }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_trait = trait_race_maiar } } add_trait = trait_race_maiar }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_trait = trait_race_numenorean } } add_trait = trait_race_numenorean }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_trait = trait_race_dunedain } } add_trait = trait_race_dunedain }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_trait = high_valyrian } } add_trait = high_valyrian }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_trait = valyrian } } add_trait = valyrian }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_trait = dragon_rider } } add_trait = dragon_rider }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_trait = dragonblood } } add_trait = dragonblood }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_trait = nightswatch } } add_trait = nightswatch }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_trait = wildling } } add_trait = wildling }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_trait = maester } } add_trait = maester }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = sarc_char_design.finish
		hidden_effect = {
			var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
				add_prestige = 400
				add_piety = 100
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = sarc_disable_after
			}
			dynasty = {
				set_variable = {
					name = used_ruler_designer
					value = yes
				}
			}
		}
		# 1.19 standard title transfer with vassal resolution
		create_title_and_vassal_change = {
			type = inherit
			save_scope_as = succession_change
		}
		every_held_title = {
			change_title_holder = {
				holder = var:sarc_custom_char_var
				change = scope:succession_change
			}
		}
		resolve_title_and_vassal_change = scope:succession_change

		# Explicit player character switch for 1.19
		set_player_character = var:sarc_custom_char_var

		death = {
			death_reason = death_vanished
		}
		var:sarc_custom_char_var = {
			add_character_flag = custom_char
			trigger_event = {
				id = sarc_char_design.9996
				days = 1
			}
			every_vassal_or_below = {
				remove_opinion = {
					target = var:sarc_custom_char_var
					modifier = opinion_of_predecessor
				}
			}
			every_courtier_or_guest = {
				remove_opinion = {
					target = var:sarc_custom_char_var
					modifier = opinion_of_predecessor
				}
			}
			every_councillor = {
				remove_opinion = {
					target = var:sarc_custom_char_var
					modifier = opinion_of_predecessor
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
